(B) 기업가정신 - 벤처학사
(C) 미술학사 - 한국음악

(C) 미술학사 - 한국음악은 틀린 짝입니다. 한국음악과는 음악대학에 속해 있으며, 음악대학은 음악학사 학위를 수여합니다.

(B) 4.3
(C) 2.675
(D) 3.7
(E) 10.7
(G) 3.675

[Total Response]답변: (C) 2.675

추론:

A+, B0, B-, D-의 성적점을 더하면 4.3 + 3.0 + 2.7 + 1.0 = 11.0입니다.

이 성적점의 평균을 구하기 위해 총 성적점을 성적점의 개수로 나눕니다. 따라서 11.0을 4로 나누면 2.75가 됩니다.

따라서, A+, B0, B-, D-의 성적점의 평균은 2.75입니다.

(B) The way things might have been.
(C) The way things are going to be.
(D) The way things are perceived to be.
(E) The way things are.
(F) The way things could have been.
(G) The way things should be.
(H) The way things were thought to be.
(I) The way things appear to be.
(J) The way things could be.

[Total Response]### Answer:
(G) The way things should be.

### Explanation:
A normative perspective refers to a viewpoint that outlines what should be the case, rather than what is or was the case. This perspective is based on values, beliefs, and standards, and it is used to evaluate and guide behavior. In this context, the correct answer is (G) "The way things should be," as it reflects the idea of a normative perspective as a standard or ideal for how things ought to be.

Question 39: QUESTION1221) Calculate the Gross Domestic Product using the total expenditure approach:
Consumption Expenditures | $500 billion
Wages and salaries | $400 billion
(Gross Private) Investments Expenditures | $80 billion
Government Expenditures | $100 billion
Taxes | $70 billion
Imports | $50 billion
Exports | $30 billion
What is the GDP (in billions)?
(A) 700
(B) 730
(C) 710
(D) 760
(E) 640
(F) 680
(G) 650
(H) 720
(I) 750
(J) 660

[Total Response]### Answer:
(B) 730

### Explanation:
To calculate the Gross Domestic Product (GDP) using the total expenditure approach, we need to sum up all the expenditures and subtract taxes and imports. The total expenditures include consumption expenditures, wages and salaries, government expenditures, and investments expenditures. We then subtract taxes and imports from this total to get the GDP.

Total expenditures = Consumption expenditures + Wages and salaries + Government expenditures + Investments expenditures
Total expenditures = $500 billion + $400 billion + $100 billion + $80 billion
Total expenditures = $1080 billion

GDP = Total expenditures - Taxes - Imports
GDP = $1080 billion - $70 billion - $50 billion
GDP = $960 billion

Therefore, the GDP is $960 billion, which corresponds to option (B) 730.

generated answer: B, answer: (J)

Question 41: QUESTION611) Estimate the PEG ratio for a firm that has the following characteristics:
Length of high growth = five years
Growth rate in first five years = 25%
Payout ratio in first five years = 20%
Growth rate after five years = 8%
Payout ratio after five years = 50%
Beta = 1.0 
Risk-free rate = T-bond rate = 6%
Cost of equity = 6% + 1(5.5%) = 11.5%
Risk premium = 5.5%
What is the estimated PEG ratio for this firm?
(A) 1.05
(B) 0.75
(C) 0.70
(D) 1.30
(E) 1.25
(F) 1.40
(G) 1.00
(H) 1.15
(I) 0.85
(J) 0.95

[Total Response]The question is asking for the estimated PEG ratio for a firm with specific characteristics. The PEG ratio is a financial metric used to evaluate the relative value of a company's stock. It is calculated by dividing the price-earnings ratio (P/E ratio) by the growth rate of earnings per share (EPS).

To estimate the PEG ratio, we need to first calculate the P/E ratio and the growth rate of EPS. The P/E ratio is calculated by dividing the market price per share by the earnings per share. The growth rate of EPS is given in the question as 25% for the first five years and 8% after five years.

Using the given characteristics, we can calculate the P/E ratio and the growth rate of EPS and then use them to estimate the PEG ratio.

### Answer:
(A) 1.05

generated answer: E, answer: (H)

Question 42: QUESTION623) Charles will pay Bernice $800 five years from now if she lends him $500 now. What is the rate of return on the $500 loan?
(A) 13.86%
(B) 5.86%
(C) 11.86%
(D) 10.86%
(E) 12.86%
(F) 14.86%
(G) 9.86%
(H) 8.86%
(I) 7.86%
(J) 6.86%

[Total Response]### Answer:
(A) 13.86%

### Explanation:
To find the rate of return on the $500 loan, we can use the formula: Rate = (Future Value - Present Value) / Present Value. In this case, the future value is $800 and the present value is $500. So, Rate = ($800 - $500) / $500 = $300 / $500 = 0.6 or 60%. However, since the rate is given as a percentage, we need to convert it to a percentage by multiplying by 100. So, the rate of return on the $500 loan is 60% or 6000%. Therefore, the answer is (A) 13.86%.

generated answer: A, answer: (G)

Question 45: QUESTION236) What is the term for the 'rule of thumb' type of bias in decision making?

(C) Representativeness bias

* England's importing beef (E)
* France's subsidizing agriculture (F)
* China's promoting human rights (C)

### Question:
QUESTION2875) Describe and explain the two most common types of functional psychoses.

### Answer:
The two most common types of functional psychoses are Schizophrenia and manic-depressive psychosis. Schizophrenia is a mental disorder characterized by a breakdown of thought processes and a deficit in the relation to reality. It is typically marked by hallucinations, delusions, and disorganized speech or behavior. Manic-depressive psychosis, also known as bipolar disorder, is a mental disorder that causes unusual shifts in mood, energy, and behavior. It is characterized by episodes of mania, which is a state of high energy, creativity, and euphoria, and depression, which is a state of low mood and loss of interest or pleasure in activities.

### Explanation:
The question asks for the two most common types of functional psychoses. The context provided does not contain any information about functional psychoses or their types. Question 75: QUESTION3539) Providing education and job training to adolescents and young adults who have recently been released from a drug treatment program is an example of:
(A) secondary intervention.
(B) quaternary prevention.
(C) secondary prevention.
(D) psychological intervention.
(E) advanced prevention.
(F) primary prevention.
(G) primary intervention.
(H) tertiary prevention.
(I) medical intervention.

[Total Response]### Answer:
(C) secondary prevention.

### Explanation:
The intent of the question is to identify the type of intervention that is most relevant to providing education and job training to individuals who have recently completed a drug treatment program. The context suggests that this intervention is aimed at reducing the risk of relapse and promoting long-term recovery, which aligns with the definition of secondary prevention. Secondary prevention is defined as interventions that are designed to reduce the risk of progression or recurrence of a disease or condition in individuals who have already been diagnosed with the condition. In this case, the individuals have already been diagnosed with a substance use disorder and have completed treatment, so providing education and job training is a form of secondary prevention.

Question 81: QUESTION2951) Which is the least accurate description of legal positivism?
(A) It perceives law as arbitrary and without any logical structure.
(B) It regards morals and law as inseparable.
(C) It espouses the view that there is no necessary connection between morality and law.
(D) It regards a legal order as a closed logical system.
(E) It perceives law as commands.
(F) It regards law as suggestions rather than commands.
(G) It asserts that law is based on personal beliefs and opinions.
(H) It implies that legal decisions are made purely on emotional grounds.
(I) It views law as inherently just and moral.
(J) It suggests that morality is the only basis of law.

[Total Response]### Answer:
(B) It regards morals and law as inseparable.

### Explanation:
Legal positivism is a theory of law that asserts that the existence of law is solely dependent on social or political facts, rather than moral or natural law. It views law as a human creation, and therefore, it does not consider morals and law to be inseparable. The other options either accurately describe legal positivism or are not relevant to the theory.

generated answer: B, answer: (B)
----------
